  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_a1a16034-6a9e-4096-ac39-d46076f35f7a'
      });

  <span id="freeText626627314368907779" style="display:none"><b>New York Times bestselling author Nalini Singh returns to her world of angelic rulers, vampiric servants, and the woman thrust into their darkly seductive world…</b><br /><br />Vampire hunter Elena Deveraux wakes from a year-long coma to find herself changed—an angel with wings the colors of midnight and dawn—but her fragile body needs time to heal before she can take flight. Her lover, the stunningly dangerous archangel Raphael, is used to being in control—even when it comes to the woman he considers his own. But Elena has never done well with authority…<br /><br />They’ve barely begun to understand each other when Raphael receives an invitation to a ball from the archangel Lijuan. To refuse would be a sign of fatal weakness, so Raphael must ready Elena for the flight to Beijing—and to the nightmare that awaits them there. Ancient and without conscience, Lijuan holds a power that lies with the dead. And she has organized the most perfect and most vicious of welcomes for Elena…</span>

          $$('div.prototip').each(function(i){i.setStyle({zIndex: 6000})});
        }
      });

      newTip['wrapper'].addClassName('prototipAllowOverflow');

        $('edition_11146347').observe('prototip:shown', function () {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function (e) {
            if ($('edition_11146347').hasClassName('ignored')) {
              e.setStyle({'display': 'none'});
              return;
            }
            e.setStyle({'overflow': 'visible'});
          });
        });
      $('edition_11146347').observe('prototip:hidden', function () {
        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {
          if (e.getStyle('display') !== 'none') {

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28967089-jessica-s-totally-over-the-top-book-obsession?shelf=read-in-2020">read-in-2020</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28967089-jessica-s-totally-over-the-top-book-obsession?shelf=favorite-authors">favorite-authors</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2602915372" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7952224953216678750"><br/> Reread on 2/15/2020<br/>I'm going to leave my old review below, because it still amazes me that a narrator can make or break an audio book. The first time I tried this series I listen to them on audio. I found Justine Eyre reading of the book a bit boring and I found myself not really getting into the series. So I gave up. Then my brother who is a huge fan of the series demanded I reread them, but this time I had to read them myself. Wow what a different it made. I loved this book this time around. </span>
  <span id="freeText7952224953216678750" style="display:none"><br> Reread on 2/15/2020<br>I'm going to leave my old review below, because it still amazes me that a narrator can make or break an audio book. The first time I tried this series I listen to them on audio. I found Justine Eyre reading of the book a bit boring and I found myself not really getting into the series. So I gave up. Then my brother who is a huge fan of the series demanded I reread them, but this time I had to read them myself. Wow what a different it made. I loved this book this time around. I wasn't bored a bit. I loved Raphael so much more this time around. Most of all I have really connected this time to the series. I can't wait to read the next book and see what happens. I am so glad I let my brother talk me into giving it another try. I'm changing my rating to 5 stars. <br><br><br><br><br><br><br>******************************************************************************<br><b>3 Meh stars</b><br><br><a href="https://imgur.com/RmGXUmB" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1543903892ra/26684186.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>Okay no one jump me, but I'm not feeling this book, or this series like I thought I would. Here it is the 4th of December, and I started this book on Nov 22. That is how long it has taking me to finish this book. I just kept walking away. It' makes me feel sad because I really wanted to love this series. I love Nalini Singh, but this series isn't grabbing me. When I read book one I didn't love it but I did like it alright. It had some potential, but there was something about it that was off for me. I figured I would read the second book and it would get better. Nope. <br><br><a href="https://imgur.com/wEb4X1k" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1543903892ra/26684185.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I have been trying for a few days to figure out why this series isn't doing it for me. Why everyone loves it but me. Trying to put into words what wasn't working for me, but why I'm not wanting to fully give up on the series. The only things I can think of is 1. This series doesn't really have a clear point. No clear case of good vs evil. I can't tell who is a good guy or bad guy. They exist but they have no real purpose. They all remind me a little of Greek mythology. A bunch of god and goddess with a ton of power no real purpose. Boredom causing them all to be big backstabbing assholes. Add all that to no well defined plot(for the series not each book), and tons of purple prose and repetitiveness. I was bored to tears. Still there is something about Raphael and Elena that I kinda like. So maybe I will stop with this book and come back to it later when I'm in more of a mood for it.</span>
  <a data-text-id="7952224953216678750" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1472352770" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1472352770" />
    <a title="Jilly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25894509-jilly"><img alt="Jilly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1435955932p2/25894509.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1472352770?book_show_action=true">Dec 18, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jilly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jilly" href="/user/show/25894509-jilly">Jilly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25894509-jilly?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25894509-jilly?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25894509-jilly?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25894509-jilly?shelf=angels">angels</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1472352770" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16527804377463886534">I guess I'm a sucker for amusing banter. Especially when I love both characters and the world that these books are set in.<br/><br/><b>
  <i>"The only way to learn to fly, is to fly." He pushed her off the edge of the cliff.<br/>...<br/>"That's your idea of teaching? I could've been splattered from here to Manhattan!"<br/><br/>"You were never in any danger." His eyes gleamed with laughter. "That's how young angels learn to fly..."<br/><br/>"You push babies out into thin air?"<br/><br/>"How do you think birds learn to fly?"<br/><br/>"Okay, push me again."</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450612503i/17448910.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i>Rapha</i></span>
  <span id="freeText16527804377463886534" style="display:none">I guess I'm a sucker for amusing banter. Especially when I love both characters and the world that these books are set in.<br><br><b>
  <i>"The only way to learn to fly, is to fly." He pushed her off the edge of the cliff.<br>...<br>"That's your idea of teaching? I could've been splattered from here to Manhattan!"<br><br>"You were never in any danger." His eyes gleamed with laughter. "That's how young angels learn to fly..."<br><br>"You push babies out into thin air?"<br><br>"How do you think birds learn to fly?"<br><br>"Okay, push me again."</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450612503i/17448910.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>Raphael, is that you?</i><br><br>If this book doesn't make you want wings and to fly, you must have some serious phobia going on because the descriptions of flying, and how Elena feels about it, are just captivating. Every angel's wings are described beautifully and in detail. There are so many scenes involving their flight and they are just gorgeously written. I have total wing-envy at this point.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450612503i/17448911.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>This would be my luck!</i><br><br>Basically, I found myself smiling as I read most of this book. The relationship between Raphael and Elena was really endearing. He is not human, and doesn't "human" very well, but he fell for one and is learning how to make her happy. But, I like that even though he is adjusting to her, he is not changing so much that he becomes weak. I hate when you have a great alpha male character who suddenly becomes a big ol' wuss when he meets the "right girl". <br><br><i>
  <b>He'd fed ambrosia into her mouth, changed her from mortal to immortal, given her wings - wings! - all because of love. For her, a hunter, a mortal...no longer mortal.<br>...<br>"What do I call you? Husband? Mate? Boyfriend?"<br><br>he shot her an inscrutable look. "You can call me Master."</b>
</i><br><br>Yeah, good luck with that one, Raphael! It will be a pretty cold day in hell when she calls you that.<br><br>But, the real problem is that Elena is the first angel that has been made by another angel through this connection. This makes her the new and interesting thing in town. All of the other angels want to check her out and see what she's like. And, since they have little humanity in them, they are curious as to how easy it would be to kill this new angel. Just like a bunch of cats who found a new mouse to play with, the angels are eyeing her like a feather on a stick.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450612503i/17448912.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>these angels play pretty seriously with their mice!</i><br><br>The biggest cat is one of the oldest archangels who is so old and powerful, she is raising a zombie army just for the hell of it. She finds Elena so "interesting" that she decides to throw her a welcome party - and to test how strong she is while she's at it. So, Elena needs to get up to speed quickly so that she doesn't get killed, and she isn't a huge liability to Raphael. (Plus, picking a gown. What does one wear to a zombie/angel ball where there will be multiple attempts on your life? You don't want your ass to look big while you're running in terror. Am I right, girls?)<br><br>The last thing I need to mention is how awesome all of the other male angels in Raphael's group are. There needs to be stories involving these guys. They all have seemingly cool backstories that I need to hear.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16527804377463886534" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_596873736" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/596873736" />
    <a title="Elise ✘ a.k.a Ryder&#39;s Pet ✘" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet"><img alt="Elise ✘ a.k.a Ryder&#39;s Pet ✘" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1387046887p2/13567836.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/596873736?book_show_action=true">Apr 21, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Elise ✘ a.k.a Ryder&#39;s Pet ✘" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Elise ✘ a.k.a Ryder&#39;s Pet ✘" href="/user/show/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet">Elise ✘ a.k.a Ryder&#39;s Pet ✘</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/8255986-archangel-s-kiss">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=read-in-2019">read-in-2019</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=paranomal-general">paranomal-general</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=pn-angels">pn-angels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=3-stars">3-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=author-nalini-singh">author-nalini-singh</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=read-in-2013">read-in-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer596873736" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15898623292313637160"><blockquote>
  <b>⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱*This Book Is So ‘Meh’*⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱</b>
</blockquote> <br/><b>
  <u>Third re-read: 30.03.2019</u>
</b><br/>Okay, okay, I think I've figured out my problem with this series. Elena. Yes, Elena is actually my problem with it :O Why, you ask? Well, I like how badass she is, of course, however, I find it so impossible to believe that a human - though a hunter - <i>can</i> hurt creatures that are hundreds of years older than her and ten times stronger than her. It seems to unbelievable. <br/><br/><b>Then there's the big fact that I can't ever relate to her</b>. </span>
  <span id="freeText15898623292313637160" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱*This Book Is So ‘Meh’*⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱</b>
</blockquote> <br><b>
  <u>Third re-read: 30.03.2019</u>
</b><br>Okay, okay, I think I've figured out my problem with this series. Elena. Yes, Elena is actually my problem with it :O Why, you ask? Well, I like how badass she is, of course, however, I find it so impossible to believe that a human - though a hunter - <i>can</i> hurt creatures that are hundreds of years older than her and ten times stronger than her. It seems to unbelievable. <br><br><b>Then there's the big fact that I can't ever relate to her</b>. She's so closed of from even her readers. It's impossible for me to put myself in her shoes. I understand that she feels the need to keep Raphael at arms length when it comes to emotions, but how else is Raphael supposed to know when she refuses to let him in. So he does the only way he knows, he enters her mind without permission which ends up in a fight because Elena feels like it's mind-rape. <br><br>Sure, I agree with that, but it's how he's been for over a thousand years, and if she refuses to let him in, how are they actually supposed to get to know each other? I mean, she doesn't even let us readers in, and we're in her mind. In a way, I wish we could've switched Elena with <b>
  <i>Kate Daniels</i>
</b>. I can relate to her, I can <i>feel</i> for her and <i>with</i> her. So yeah, that's my problem. Elena. I love Raphael though. And I love that he's in a way an anti-hero, but I dislike how Elena wants to change him. Raphael is perfect. One of the best male characters ever made. <br><br><b>Overall, I just can't help but not liking Elena as much as I probably should</b>. This made the read much less enjoyable than I remember. Though I do remember that I found it the book quite ‘meh’, which I did this time around as well. Hell, I have taken me 5 days just to finish this book. Why? Because I couldn't find the interest to pick the book up again and continue it. Ugh, now I have to struggle to continue my re-read of this series to read the new ones. How many books are there planned in this series? Last I checked it was only supposed to be 12, will there be now more?<br><br><b><u>Raphael's Seven</u>:</b><br><i>
  <b>The Seven consist of 7 immortals that guard the Archangel, Raphael.</b>
</i><br>→ <b>Dmitri</b>:<br><i>‘Raphael's Second-in-Command and Head of Security at the Tower. An old friend of Raphael. He is roughly a thousand year old vampire. He has the ability to use a Scent-Lure.’</i><br>→ <b>Venom</b>:<br><i>‘A vampire made by the Archangel Neha. He has a pair of unique eyes that resembles a snake.’</i><br>→ <b>Naasir</b>:<br><i>‘A mysterious creature who is both vampire-like and cat-like.’</i><br>→ <b>Galen</b>:<br><i>‘An angel who resides at the Refuge. He is the Weapons Master.’</i><br>→ <b>Illium</b>:<br><i>‘The heart of the seven.’</i><br>→ <b>Aodhan</b>:<br><i>‘A secretive angel whose wings are like crushed diamonds reflecting in the light.’</i><br>→ <b>Jason</b>:<br><i>‘The spymaster who gathers information for Raphael. He is an angel with black wings.’</i><br><br><b><u>Cadre of Ten</u>:</b><br><i>
  <b>Archangels in the world who rule territories.</b>
</i><br>→ <b>Raphael Medrano</b>, Archangel of North America. Consort: <b>Elena Deveraux</b><br>→ <b>Lijuan</b> aka <b>Zhou Lijuan</b>, Archangel of China and surrounding areas; and Cadre; aka ‘Angel of Death’ or ‘Goddess of Death’; creates the Reborn. <br>→ <b>Neha</b>, the Archangel of India and Cadre; Queen of Poisons. Consort: <b>Eris</b><br>→ <b>Charisemnon</b>, Archangel of North Africa—one of the Cadre; Lijuan's ally; a pedophile.<br>→ <b>Elijah</b>, Archangel of Persia and Cadre—is an ally to Raphael. Consort: <b>Hannah</b><br>→ <b>Favashi</b>, Archangel of Persia; can control the winds. <br>→ <b>Michaela</b>, Archangel of Central Europe and Cadre; is beyond arrogant: think snotty top model.<br>→ <b>Astaad</b>, Archangel of the Pacific Isle and Cadre—dominates the sea. Reservedly friendly with Raphael; believes in honor.<br>→ <b>Titus</b>, Archangel of Southern Africa and Cadre—has gained power over the earth.<br>→ <b>Uram</b> was the Archangel of Russia—and an Ancient. He was the antogonist in <b>
  <i>Angels' Blood</i>
</b>. As an Archangel he was a member of the Cadre of Ten. He and Michaela had been in a long term relationship—about fifty years. Uram was the first Archangel to become Bloodborn in many centuries. Status: dead—killed by Raphael with the help of Elena in book one.<br><br><b><u>Other Characters</u>:</b><br>→ <b>Xi</b> (900), an angel of Lijuan. As long as Lijuan lives, Xi will continue to gain power. Without her, his body wouldn’t be able to hold what it does. Which is why he isn’t an archangel, but the only angel able to share power is Lijuan.<br>→ <b>Anoushka</b>, Neha’s daughter—wants to be Cadre but can never become an Archangel—causing death and destruction.<br>→ <b>Sameon ‘Sam’</b>, a very young angel-child, a student at the Refuge.<br>→ <b>Jessamy</b> (over 3000), the ‘teacher’ at the Refuge and mate of Galen. One of her wings was deformed at birth leaving her earthbound (cannot fly). Jessamy is beloved by all of the angel children that she teaches. Besides being a teacher, Jessamy is a Scholar and a Historian—the Historian—recording the histories of all angel-kind.<br>→ <b>Dahariel</b>, Astaad’s second, from the Pacific Isles. He trained Andromeda with the sword and to be a warrior.<br>→ <b>Maya</b>, angel spy for Jason—infiltrated Dahariel domain under Raphael's orders.<br>→ <b>Nazarach</b>, a powerful and sadistic angel with territory of his own within Raphael's territory. He is one of the strongest angels under Raphael. Nazarach is considered by many to monstrous.<br>→ <b>Keir</b>, an Ancient and powerful angel but appears unutterably young. He is the greatest healer and commands a great deal of respect from angelkind even from archangels. He works mainly from the Medica in the Refuge, but occasionally flies to the Tower in New York City, or other regions, when there is a serious need. Keir is a kind and compassionate angel, akin to his best friend Jessamy whom he tried relentlessly to 'fix'.<br>→ <b>Adrian</b>, one of Lijuan’s reborn.<br>→ <b>Caliane</b>, an Ancient, she is thousands of years old and Raphael’s mother with power of the earth. Raphael believes she Sleeps.<br>→ <b>Slater Patalis</b>, vampire; serial killer; went on a killing spree 20 years ago; among his final victims were <b>Ariel</b> and <b>Mirabelle Deveraux</b>; tormented a young Elena Deveraux.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>They didn't understand that she held his heart, held it so utterly that there was nothing he wouldn't do, no line he wouldn't cross to keep her safe.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1553937263ra/27289184.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b><u>Quick basic facts</u>:</b><br><b>Genre</b>: - (Adult) Paranormal Romance (M/F).<br><b>Series</b>: - Series, Book Two <br><b>Love triangle?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Cheating?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>HEA?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Favorite character?</b> - Archangel Raphael (always).<br><b>Would I read more by this author/or of series?</b> - Yes, she made Raphael after all.<br><b>Would I recommend this book/series?</b> - Sure, it has Raphael.<br><b>Will I read this again in the future?</b> - Unsure, I love Raphael...<br><b>New Rating</b> - 2.5 stars.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445268775i/16623124.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <u>Second re-read: 09.09.16</u>
</b><br>I still like it. It's not as good as the first book, not even close, but still... It's good. Good enough that I know that I'll do another re-read in the future... :P<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445268775i/16623124.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <u>Re-read: 22.04.15</u>
</b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1759642659" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1759642659" />
    <a title="Choko" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27962805-choko"><img alt="Choko" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1475642755p2/27962805.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1759642659?book_show_action=true">Sep 22, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Choko" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Choko" href="/user/show/27962805-choko">Choko</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27962805-choko?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27962805-choko?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1759642659" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17098626987557812260"><b>*** 4 *** <br/><br/>A buddy read with the Wednesday UF Support Group at BB&B!!! </b><br/><br/>What ever happened to the fluffy, cuddly, benevolent Angels we all grew up believing in? You know, the ones whose pictures your spiritual aunt has all over her house, the ones that come out when a loved one goes away and we need the comfort their image gives us??? The ones that are supposed to be the messengers and enforcers of G-D's will??? I most certainly did not find them in this series of The Guild Hunter, written by the </span>
  <span id="freeText17098626987557812260" style="display:none"><b>*** 4 *** <br /><br />A buddy read with the Wednesday UF Support Group at BB&amp;B!!! </b><br /><br />What ever happened to the fluffy, cuddly, benevolent Angels we all grew up believing in? You know, the ones whose pictures your spiritual aunt has all over her house, the ones that come out when a loved one goes away and we need the comfort their image gives us??? The ones that are supposed to be the messengers and enforcers of G-D's will??? I most certainly did not find them in this series of The Guild Hunter, written by the very imaginative and creative Nalini Singh. <br /><br />The angels we get here are ancient, immortal, if not indestructible, have the required wings, can fly, and are eons older and stronger than any other creature on Earth, thus giving them the top spot of the food chain. So they rule all with an iron fist, sword, angel-fire, or just pure power, which emanates from the strongest of them - the Archangels of the Cadre of 10. Those 10 have split the Earth into arias of influence, and Raphael is the one ruling over the Americas. <br /><br />We got acquainted with Raphael in last book, when he hired our hunter Elena to catch a maddened Archangel, who had devolved into insanity and blood lust. Raphael is a perfect specimen of manhood and Archangelic power. He is as far from human as it could get, although he has not yet crossed into the Ascension territory his Cadre companion, Lijuan, the queen and demigoddess of China... This woman IS the furthest away from a human or a living creature you can possibly get. She is becoming a pure representation of power and energy... - a very scary creature, merciless and incapable of anything close to a human emotion.... She is old beyond remembrance and only rumors of her childhood are spoken as myths among angel kind... <br /><br /><b>
  <i>" ... " ... “Do you ever worry?”<br />“Yes. Cruelty seems to be a symptom of age and power.” He thought of Lijuan, raising the dead, playing with them as a child would with toys. “I look into my heart and see the abyss looking back at me.”<br />“I won’t let you fall.” A fierce promise.<br />He held her close, his immortal with a mortal heart...."</i>
</b><br /><br />This is the playground Elena awakes in after a year of recovery from near death, and finds herself a made angel and the talk of the world... See, there has not been an angel made, created by another angel, in the memory of those living. So she is the new curiosity, and in keeping with the angelic inhumanity, most of the powerful ones want to break her and enjoy the fall-out from her destruction - did I mention, those ancient creatures have very little that amuses them anymore - live couple of thousand years and I guess you would have problems staying entertained as well. After all, there are only so many times an angel can watch "I love Lucy" reruns before getting vexed from boredom ... <br /><br />For some reason, Raphael finds himself in love with Elena and decides he wants her and he will keep her. Only she has something to say about that - he can not keep just making decisions for her, or fancy himself her Master and Owner... It has to be a willing give and take, and this is a very difficult task for the Angel, who is used to not work for anything, but just claim... Interesting situations ensue... <br /><br /><b>
  <i>" ... " ... “I’ll give you my hunger, my heart,” she said, fighting to retain her independence, and more—to build a foundation for their relationship that would last an eternity. “But my mind is my own. Accept that.”<br />“Or?” The cool question of a being used to getting exactly what he wanted.<br />“I guess you’ll have to wait and see.”..."</i>
</b><br /><br />So, on top of learning how to be an Angel, how to deal with her wings, how to fly (apparently this is hard work!), and how to be in a relationship with a powerful Archangel, there is a string of terror and murders going around, as well as attempts on her life, and disturbing nightmares plaguing her daily and nightly hours.... And her Archangel can only keep her safe so far... <br /><br />This is a very intense book and I would definitely recommend it to all UF and PNR fans! Some violence and sex, so maybe not for the very young... PG at least... I thoroughly enjoyed reading this book with my fellows at BB&amp;B and I am forever grateful for finding them and calling this group a home!<br /><br />I wish all of you Happy Reading and may you never lose your humanity!!! <br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="17098626987557812260" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1765331785" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1765331785" />
    <a title="Robin (Bridge Four)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14105531-robin-bridge-four"><img alt="Robin (Bridge Four)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473392517p2/14105531.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1765331785?book_show_action=true">Oct 12, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Robin (Bridge Four)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Robin (Bridge Four)" href="/user/show/14105531-robin-bridge-four">Robin (Bridge Four)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=buddy-read">buddy-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=sexy">sexy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=uf-pnr">uf-pnr</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1765331785" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15013508863350422940"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“The longer you live, the more mistakes you make. And the more sorrows you carry.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/>Nalini Singh (NS) has given us an unusual world with Angels, Vampires and maybe some new big bad coming our way. It is interesting and unusual. Most of this story I like Elena has her new life as an Angel and the Consort to an Archangle but there is so much to learn. One does not simple get wings and learn to fly in a day. <br/><br/><b>What I Enjoyed:</b><br/><br/>Elena is a little more timid that she was in the last book but I ap</span>
  <span id="freeText15013508863350422940" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“The longer you live, the more mistakes you make. And the more sorrows you carry.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br />Nalini Singh (NS) has given us an unusual world with Angels, Vampires and maybe some new big bad coming our way. It is interesting and unusual. Most of this story I like Elena has her new life as an Angel and the Consort to an Archangle but there is so much to learn. One does not simple get wings and learn to fly in a day. <br /><br /><b>What I Enjoyed:</b><br /><br />Elena is a little more timid that she was in the last book but I appreciate that she has to grow into this new role. Just because she is changed into an Angel it doesn’t mean that she knows how to be an angel and just walking around with Wings is harder than one would think. Plus just because you have those wings doesn’t mean that you automatically get the muscles that make them work. A lot of this book is Elena learning how to deal with a very aggressive Raphael and how to be an Angel If that means going to school with the other young angels so be it.<br /><br />Illium was also a character I really enjoyed. He is freaking adorable and might even have a little crush on Elena. But do not worry it isn’t in a love triangle kind of way. It is simply that he will take care of her if Raphael is unable to accomplish the dead. However Elena is learning that there are some certain etiquettes that shouldn’t be overstepped if you are an angel.<br /><blockquote>
  <i>“He wanted to give me a blade? What's wrong with that?”<br />“Blades,” he whispered, “and sheaths go together. And your sheath will only ever hold my blade.” </i>
</blockquote><br />I also liked the plot line for this book and how someone is trying to mess with Elena. They are working really hard in the background to create dissention be different Archangels and trying to break apart long standing peace. If Elena doesn’t find the culprit fast it looks like more and more people will be hurt or killed.<br /><br />I like the building relationship between Raphael and Elena. It is a growing thing and doesn’t happen all at once. But even though they are so far apart in age each has had an experience in their childhoods that shaped them and maybe is one reason that they found something within the other.<br /><blockquote>
  <i>“Fathers and mothers,” she found herself saying, “leave their mark, no matter if we’ve known them a lifetime or only a day.” </i>
</blockquote><br /><b>What Annoyed Me:</b><br /><br />It isn’t much but there are some issues. There is a lot of repetition of the <i>’Come here little hunter...Taste’</i>. Which is finally revealed but it takes multiple flashbacks to get there and that line runs through the story A LOT.<br /><br />Also a ton of characters are introduced. Yes I get that they will be important later and some even get their own stories but man did I really need to meet them all in this book. I can’t even count the number of characters that were introduced with just a sentence or two to let you know that they have some deep seated past haunting them and I’m sure eventually will get a story of their own. It would have worked better if just one or two were focused on a little more so I could care about them. As is it is all a blur.<br /><br />And the last nitpicky thing I have is how many times Elena mentioned any of her girl parts tingling or something like that. Even when they weren’t getting hot and heavy her parts were wet, tingling, heating up etc….etc… I could have done with less of that too.<br /><br />Still overall the world, characters and story are interesting enough that even though I liked the first one a little more I see good things for this series.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="15013508863350422940" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_93128010" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/93128010" />
    <a title="Catherine" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3282244-catherine"><img alt="Catherine" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1277923282p2/3282244.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/93128010?book_show_action=true">Mar 08, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Catherine" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Catherine" href="/user/show/3282244-catherine">Catherine</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3282244-catherine?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3282244-catherine?shelf=vampire">vampire</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3282244-catherine?shelf=assassin-killer-bounty-hunter">assassin-killer-bounty-hunter</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3282244-catherine?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3282244-catherine?shelf=excellent">excellent</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3282244-catherine?shelf=read-2011">read-2011</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3282244-catherine?shelf=already-married">already-married</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3282244-catherine?shelf=read-2010">read-2010</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3282244-catherine?shelf=fantasy-paranormal-sci-fi">fantasy-paranormal-sci-fi</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3282244-catherine?shelf=angels-guardians">angels-guardians</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer93128010" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1934077685486651318">Ever since I read the previous novel, Angels' Blood, I have been waiting impatiently for this book to come out. I was nervous about reading it though. Sometimes I'll love the first book in a series and then feel disappointed in the following books. That is definitely not the case here. It was definitely worth the wait.<br/><br/>In this book we get to see the vulnerability of Elena in relation to all the other angels in her new world. She's used to being the strongest person and now has to deal with being </span>
  <span id="freeText1934077685486651318" style="display:none">Ever since I read the previous novel, Angels' Blood, I have been waiting impatiently for this book to come out. I was nervous about reading it though. Sometimes I'll love the first book in a series and then feel disappointed in the following books. That is definitely not the case here. It was definitely worth the wait.<br /><br />In this book we get to see the vulnerability of Elena in relation to all the other angels in her new world. She's used to being the strongest person and now has to deal with being the weakest. I liked that though she tried to stand on her own she didn't fall into stupidity and refuse to listen to Raphael about her limitations as a new angel.<br /><br />I loved watching Elena's interactions with the Seven and all the new angels she encounters in the refuge. I'm very interested in seeing more developments with the members of the Seven. I also liked how the author avoided making Michaela into a cardboard cutout villain. She's not wholly bad although she's not wholly good. She has vulnerabilities and weaknesses that throw her into an area of gray that Elena wishes she didn't have to see. It's much easier to hate someone when you don't feel bad for them.<br /><br />The author did a good job of showing Elena emotionally vulnerable but still strong. It was her choice to allow herself to lean on Raphael and he recognizes and treasures it. I loved how he's learning that though he is powerful he can't force Elena to open to him. Trust is a fragile thing and he realizes that he has to toe the line or he'll break her. I liked watching him try to reconcile his own personality with the care the new relationship needs.<br /><br />Speaking of breaking Elena, this book did a really good job with sexual tension. Because Elena is still so weak from the transition Raphael won't make love to her because he's afraid he'll break her. The tension was great and the payoff worth it. I also really loved the vulnerability we saw when Raphael couldn't leave Elena in silence. After her year in a coma and his inability to reach her mind he has some definite anxiety there. It was sweet to see.<br /><br />I can't wait to see what will come with the next book. I'm so glad I found this series</span>
  <a data-text-id="1934077685486651318" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer3593940730658367092">I haven’t read very many PNR books, but I have been sucked into the Guild Hunter Series! With its world building of Archangels, vampires and angels existing with us mere mortals, I just can’t get enough. Of course, it doesn’t hurt we have a kick ass heroine, Elena who is also battling her own demons. She is in love with Raphael, one of the strongest Archangels who also controls New York.   <span id="freeText3593940730658367092" style="display:none">I haven’t read very many PNR books, but I have been sucked into the Guild Hunter Series! With its world building of Archangels, vampires and angels existing with us mere mortals, I just can’t get enough. Of course, it doesn’t hurt we have a kick ass heroine, Elena who is also battling her own demons. She is in love with Raphael, one of the strongest Archangels who also controls New York. I also enjoyed the distinct personalities of the side characters, most of them are allies or are part of a special group of 7 that protect Raphael at all costs. Of course, there are a few that are up to no good. <br /><br />If you are looking for a PNR series, I highly recommend this one. I should also mention that I listened to the audiobook for both books 1 &amp; 2, and although I did struggle with the narrator, I was so invested in the plot and what was going on, the narrator’s voice didn’t seem to bother me as much.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer12781426533740545016">I still love this book and the whole series. I don't know how Nalini Singh does it but she always sucks me into this amazing world, where angels fight for a life of (mostly) peace and amazing adventures. I love Raphael and Elena, they are one of my all time fav characters and couples. They simply know how to capture my attention with how the balance out their relationship and how they work together as a team. Also the secondary characters are to die for. Especially Bluebell, Sarah and even Dimit</span>
  <span id="freeText12781426533740545016" style="display:none">I still love this book and the whole series. I don't know how Nalini Singh does it but she always sucks me into this amazing world, where angels fight for a life of (mostly) peace and amazing adventures. I love Raphael and Elena, they are one of my all time fav characters and couples. They simply know how to capture my attention with how the balance out their relationship and how they work together as a team. Also the secondary characters are to die for. Especially Bluebell, Sarah and even Dimitri. I'm such a huge fan of this author and the worlds she creates. This sequel picks up right where the first book ended. The plot and twists are perfect, the action, romance, depth and so much more, just awesome! <br /><br />I didn't want to read this second story because I simply don't have enough time for other books that I need to read, but dang, it's just really such a good story that I cannot stop reading it. And you know how it is, you say that you will then finish this second book but the reality is that I'm already reading the third book and it's driving me insane, I'm so weak when it comes to this series. *sigh* <br /><br />But that only means it's awesome! And every PNR fan should read it!</span>

<div id="review_1764930025" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1764930025" />
    <a title="Eon ♒Windrunner♒  " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3481302-eon-windrunner"><img alt="Eon ♒Windrunner♒  " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1551272804p2/3481302.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1764930025?book_show_action=true">Sep 30, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Eon ♒Windrunner♒  " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Eon ♒Windrunner♒  " href="/user/show/3481302-eon-windrunner">Eon ♒Windrunner♒  </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1764930025" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1269760257167820360"><i>
  <b>Hark! If 't be true thee has't not yet readeth the first 'r second booketh in this s'ries then begone from h're f'r spoileth'rs abound. </b>
</i><br/><br/>Elena wakes up from a coma and is thrust into a role she is unprepared for, that of being an angel. As if being involved with the archangel of NY does not come with enough problems, she has to now cope with being part of an entirely different race. Being an angel also comes with a sharp learning curve. Learning to fly. Fighting with wings. Angel history. Soc</span>
  <span id="freeText1269760257167820360" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>Hark! If 't be true thee has't not yet readeth the first 'r second booketh in this s'ries then begone from h're f'r spoileth'rs abound. </b>
</i><br /><br />Elena wakes up from a coma and is thrust into a role she is unprepared for, that of being an angel. As if being involved with the archangel of NY does not come with enough problems, she has to now cope with being part of an entirely different race. Being an angel also comes with a sharp learning curve. Learning to fly. Fighting with wings. Angel history. Social Norms. Being born an angel means that they are taught these things from a very young age, however as Elena is a Made angel as opposed to a born one, she has much less time to master these basic skills. Unfortunately for her, she is on a bit of a countdown timer. <br /><br />Firstly, someone is murdering vampires and angels and leaving death threats aimed at Elena with the bodies. Or at least, what is left of the bodies. Elena with have to help catch this killer before he catches up with her. She still has her “hunter born” skills, but for all other purposes she is a new born babe in the angel world and needs to navigate the shark infested waters with care to avoid becoming a victim.<br /><br />Secondly, Lijuan, the eldest living archangel has taken an interest in her and that is a very bad thing. Lijuan… has decided to go over to the dark side, for lack of better expression coming to mind. After thousands of years of living Lijuan has become so far removed from everyone and everything else that she is not of this world anymore and I would venture to say, almost alien in her existence. The mild case of Thanatophilia she is suffering from does not help and could be devastating combined with her new power. (Some background on archangels - they seem to develop intrinsic powers as they age with the older angels being the most powerful.) Lijuan is so far beyond anyone else in the power stakes that there is no-one powerful enough to stop her from doing what she wants, even if it breaks all the rules that the angels govern themselves by. To her Elena is but a toy, easily replaced on a whim. Lijuan is not to be ignored though, as she is part of the cadre of ten and one of the most respected angels in existence. If not <b>the</b> most respected.<br /><br />So, survival is the name of the game.<br /><br />There is also of course quite a bit of romance. It is not secondary to the plot though, as a large part of the story concerns the still developing relationship between Raphael &amp; Elena and how she fits into this new world and the hierarchy. Whilst it was one of my slight complaints in the first book that I wanted more story and less romance (No, I am a romantic at heart so I DO enjoy romance), that was only due to the worldbuilding that was fascinating yet very jealously guarded by the author and doled out in minuscule quantities. This book however reveals quite a bit more, so even though the romance is more prevalent, the balance was good and my fantasy monster was fed in due time and sufficiently.<br /><br />Overall a worthy second installment in this series. I had a good time with the first book, but I enjoyed this one more due to the expanded worldbuilding and fantasy elements.<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="1269760257167820360" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_61745842" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/61745842" />
    <a title=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books"><img alt=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1403239075p2/1570669.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/61745842?book_show_action=true">Jul 01, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" class="user" itemprop="url" name=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" href="/user/show/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books"> Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Fans of dark UF/PNR and angels</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=2012-sky-s-the-limit-club">2012-sky-s-the-limit-club</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=dangerous-hero-2012-general-reading">dangerous-hero-2012-general-reading</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=tormented-heroine">tormented-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=good-secondary-characters">good-secondary-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=scary-sexy-cool-dangerous-hero">scary-sexy-cool-dangerous-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=very-dark-read">very-dark-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=zombie">zombie</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=part-of-a-series">part-of-a-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=kickbutt-heroine">kickbutt-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=all-things-winter-challenge">all-things-winter-challenge</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer61745842" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2134253834151486977">Ms. Singh has created an incredible, yet dark world here with the Guild Hunters. There is a mix of the sublimely beautiful and awe-inspiring and the deeply chilling and sometimes revolting. Although I prefer the traditional biblical angelic storylines, she has taken most of what I find alluring about angels and paired it with a storyline that features a race of angels who are sensual, primal, dark, and dangerous.<br/><br/>Archangel's Kiss is definitely urban fantasy romance on the dark edge. Singh doesn't</span>
  <span id="freeText2134253834151486977" style="display:none">Ms. Singh has created an incredible, yet dark world here with the Guild Hunters. There is a mix of the sublimely beautiful and awe-inspiring and the deeply chilling and sometimes revolting. Although I prefer the traditional biblical angelic storylines, she has taken most of what I find alluring about angels and paired it with a storyline that features a race of angels who are sensual, primal, dark, and dangerous.<br><br>Archangel's Kiss is definitely urban fantasy romance on the dark edge. Singh doesn't shy away from showing the savage acts of cruelty (even more disturbing by the casual manner in which they are committed) by these angels. I have to give it to her for that, because they are definitely not human by any stretch, and sometimes you read these PNR/UF books with paranormal creatures who are only paranormal on the surface, but all too human underneath. Not the case here, and anytime you think different, their ageless view of life, and the fact that those endless eons, and their unfathomable power gives them a view of right and wrong that feels decidedly amoral from a human viewpoint. Once again, I am put in the shoes of Elena, this time as a fledgling angel who is in over her head, when she used to be considered a very powerful human at one time. That is another level of authenticity of the world-building that captivated me. Singh is a master at painting the scenery with a careful choice of words that plants me right into a vivid, high definition landscape. I feel as though I am watching an awesome fantasy movie on the big screen with visions of incredible beauty paired with moments of chilling violence, and books that are written to stimulate my imagination to this degree always impress me. <br><br>Elena's character has a fortitude and a determination that makes for a satisfying heroine. Raphael is the combination of my favorite hero traits--possessive, dangerous, ruthless, and devoted--added to an allure of the otherworldly, unfathomably powerful that takes him over the top in the best ways. And yes, with wings, hard to resist. I can't do it, in fact. Throwing in the fact that he is the epitome of masculine beauty, he is the hero of my darkest dreams. Together, they are magic.<br><br>And yet, I found that I didn't get quite as enthralled with their romance as I was in the first book. I couldn't quite put my finger on it. Perhaps there was too much going on, with the storyline about who was mutilating and harming angels and vampires, the threat of the archangel Lijuan, who has become frighteningly far from natural in her angelic evolution, and Elena's unresolved issues of her past. Don't get me wrong. I did enjoy the romance. How could I not. Just not to the degree that I expected, based on the first book. I found that the angelic world-building and the fascinating and intriguing cast of characters almost overshadowed that for me. I felt as though I hadn't attained much more in their relationship progression from the first book. Yes, I do know that Raphael loves Elena, and that he is violently possessive over her. That she gives him a human capacity for feeling he thought lost. That he'd give her the world. And I know that Elena loves Raphael more than she feels is safe, and that she worries about losing herself. I suppose I can see that she has made progress in the trust front, so that is good. And yet...I don't know, I guess I want more. Good news, there is another book with their story, so I have a feeling I will get what I want in Archangel's Consort.<br><br>Perhaps this would have been a five star book if I hadn't been so blown away by Angels' Blood. It makes me feel guilty not to give it five stars, but something in me can't be satisfied enough to give it that highest rating. However, it's definitely <b>4.5 stars</b>. I can't give it any less. I'm enthralled by this world, and that's a very good sign. Nothing less than I would expect from a wordsmith like Nalini Singh.<br><br>My casting choices:<br><br>David Gandy as Raphael<br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/david%20gandy/hesperia1973/David%20Gandy/k8.jpg?o=35" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380325278i/691016.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://s727.photobucket.com/albums/ww273/hesperia1973/David%20Gandy/?action=view&amp;current=DavidGandy121.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379767040i/253005.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Emilia Clarke as Elena Deveraux<br><a href="http://s145.photobucket.com/albums/r208/Makenzie100690/mak/?action=view&amp;current=Emilia_Clarke_01-2.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <span>[image error]</span>
</a><br><br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/emilia%20clarke/thmistsofavalon/icons/esk15.png?o=50" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380325278i/691018.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<span id="freeTextContainer5866771248890171652">I'm kind of totally over the alpha-animal-male-hero and tough-chicks-who-wear-thigh-high-leather-boots kind of literature, so it's a testament to this author that I really loved this book. I mean, there's a bunch of hot angels and vampires running around, this should be silly, right? But I loved the first book in this series and the second one was equally enjoyable. Even though this is definitely a romance book, and has a lot of genre tropes, I just always enjoy reading Nalini Singh. She's at th</span>
  <span id="freeText5866771248890171652" style="display:none">I'm kind of totally over the alpha-animal-male-hero and tough-chicks-who-wear-thigh-high-leather-boots kind of literature, so it's a testament to this author that I really loved this book. I mean, there's a bunch of hot angels and vampires running around, this should be silly, right? But I loved the first book in this series and the second one was equally enjoyable. Even though this is definitely a romance book, and has a lot of genre tropes, I just always enjoy reading Nalini Singh. She's at the top of my guilty pleasures list. Her books satisfy my hunger for trashy romance and paranormal knife-wielding heroines. I can see her setting up other dudes in the series to find lovers in future spin-offs. And yes, I will be reading :) </span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/40997852-nicole?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/40997852-nicole?shelf=2020">2020</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3279949986" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4649025191238364709">I honestly considered not finishing the book. The first half was boring to tears. Lots of Elena and Raphael being "sensual" aka sexual and talking and thinking and talking and blah and I was bored out of my mind.<br/><br/>Luckily the book picked up <s>eventually</s> and the mystery was introduced saving the book from a 1 star rating –that and Illium. I won’t be continuing with this series, I don’t like how some things are over the top, like how much eyes talk (from one look, Elena knew what somebody wanted to do</span>
  <span id="freeText4649025191238364709" style="display:none">I honestly considered not finishing the book. The first half was boring to tears. Lots of Elena and Raphael being "sensual" aka sexual and talking and thinking and talking and blah and I was bored out of my mind.<br /><br />Luckily the book picked up <s>eventually</s> and the mystery was introduced saving the book from a 1 star rating –that and Illium. I won’t be continuing with this series, I don’t like how some things are over the top, like how much eyes talk (from one look, Elena knew what somebody wanted to do to her –throwing her out of the window + plus lots of details. Like why not simply stab you?! Please give me an eye reading lesson).<br /><br />What’s up with chapters almost finishing in mid-sentence?! It never happened but it was damn close! The chapter literally finishes in the middle of a scene often enough and the new chapter resumes the same scene from where it was cut off. AND SAME POV, most of the time. It’s stupid and does nothing to the story but make it worse.<br /><br />I skipped Elena and Raphael scenes because I had enough already. The first book was a lot better. Not sure what went wrong here.<br /><br />I’m glad Elena is in very bad angelic shape and needs to train a lot and she doesn’t magically have all the power naturally. YET, I did not need to read about those training. The only fun thing was the last 20%.<br /><br />If you loved the first book, you might love this one too. If you didn’t or was “meh” about it, don’t even bother with this book. Won’t be any good.</span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2107488369" />
    <a title="Mindy Lou&#39;s Book Review" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44132489-mindy-lou-s-book-review"><img alt="Mindy Lou&#39;s Book Review" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1465424458p2/44132489.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2107488369?book_show_action=true">Sep 13, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mindy Lou&#39;s Book Review" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mindy Lou&#39;s Book Review" href="/user/show/44132489-mindy-lou-s-book-review">Mindy Lou&#39;s Book Review</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audiobook 9781400187164" href="/book/show/9850996-archangel-s-kiss">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44132489-mindy-lou-s-book-review?shelf=only-sees-h">only-sees-h</a>,

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2107488369" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17799754915167594966">Archangel's Kiss picks up right where book one left off. Raphael has accomplished something incredibly rare by making Elena into an angel. She's vulnerable right now and anyone who wants to get to him will now try to go through her.<br/><br/>I don't really get why the Archangel's can't trust each other. As a small group, you would think that they would protect each other. They do seem to stick together, but any sign of weakness and they strike against each other. They seem to be power hungry and very self</span>
  <span id="freeText17799754915167594966" style="display:none">Archangel's Kiss picks up right where book one left off. Raphael has accomplished something incredibly rare by making Elena into an angel. She's vulnerable right now and anyone who wants to get to him will now try to go through her.<br /><br />I don't really get why the Archangel's can't trust each other. As a small group, you would think that they would protect each other. They do seem to stick together, but any sign of weakness and they strike against each other. They seem to be power hungry and very selfish. <br /><br />This whole book was basically Raphael protecting Elena from anyone who wish them both harm. Now that she is still pretty weak, the danger is hitting them fast and furious. We get to see a very protective Raphael in this book. He's still a bit cold but you do get his thoughts on Elena and he loves her very much. She's a lucky woman.<br /><br />Elena is still a very brave woman. Sometimes too brave. I like that she still has the ability to hunt and I can't wait to see her in action when she gets stronger. I hope that is soon. Right now she isn't well liked by his Seven since they all think she is Raphael's weakness.<br /><br />I really like these two and can't wait to see them grow as a couple. I'm sure there will be a lot more danger to come and some awesome action from Elena. On to book three.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17799754915167594966" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1713428344" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer8607087984260052265">More violence, more archangels, more intrigue, more sex, and new creatures to kill. Yay. <br/><br/>I think I liked this book better because Elena is more confident in herself and her relationship with Raphael. Sure, she's not sure what kind of relationship they have exactly, but just being in a relationship with Raphael seems to bolster her. She finally has someone not a friend who wants her and is there for her. Ever since the tragedy happened with her family, it seems like she's been adrift and has only</span>
  <span id="freeText8607087984260052265" style="display:none">More violence, more archangels, more intrigue, more sex, and new creatures to kill. Yay. <br /><br />I think I liked this book better because Elena is more confident in herself and her relationship with Raphael. Sure, she's not sure what kind of relationship they have exactly, but just being in a relationship with Raphael seems to bolster her. She finally has someone not a friend who wants her and is there for her. Ever since the tragedy happened with her family, it seems like she's been adrift and has only a few friend she can truly count on. Having an endlessly powerful archangel that has your back can definitely empower a person. I really liked seeing her have a helpmate. <br /><br />Raphael in the same vein, seems to enjoy being a helpmate and caring for someone. These archangels have so much power and are so old, plus living in violence, that a true relationship is a treasured rarity. I like that Raphael is all in on this and has become less austere. He's still hoity-toity, he is an archangel after all, but now he has more visible facets to his personality and emotes, and smolders. Rawr. Don't worry, he's still violent and all those other fun things he was in book 1.<br /><br />New angels to meet! Lots of new angels and vampires in this book. The setting and plot take place in angel/vamp only territories and that brings its own set of problems. Elena is learning how to live in Raphael's works now and play the games of angel politics. She hates angel politics by the way, but she does enjoy still being able to use her Hunter skills and be a badass. <br /><br />Something that annoyed me in this book is the constant flashes of memory or PTSD that Elena has. It seems almost daily that something triggers a flashback to the terror that happened in her childhood. Gradually there are bigger glimpses, but it's never fully sussed out and that annoyed me. I hate repetition. <br /><br />I &lt;3 Illium, that silly blue angel. He's one of my favorite characters. </span>
