    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1703336518" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1703336518" />
    <a title="Hayley ☾ (TheVillainousReader)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/22062635-hayley-thevillainousreader"><img alt="Hayley ☾ (TheVillainousReader)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1595882462p2/22062635.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1703336518?book_show_action=true">Jul 19, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Hayley ☾ (TheVillainousReader)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Hayley ☾ (TheVillainousReader)" href="/user/show/22062635-hayley-thevillainousreader">Hayley ☾ (TheVillainousReader)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1703336518" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16111008498357216092"><b>*There are spoilers in here! I tried to hide them but it doesn't seem to work for the phone app.*</b><br/>First off, can I please exchange my boyfriend for the men in this series? Venom or Dmitri preferably but anyone will do really... <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1469674198ra/19843277.gif' width='300' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Secondly, I FOUND OUT HOW ANGELS WEAR THEIR SHIRTS! As you know from my last review this concept is really important to me and now that I've figured it out I need not read another word. Just kidding, this world is addicting. <br/><br/>I was a little unsure going into this book espec</span>
  <span id="freeText16111008498357216092" style="display:none"><b>*There are spoilers in here! I tried to hide them but it doesn't seem to work for the phone app.*</b><br>First off, can I please exchange my boyfriend for the men in this series? Venom or Dmitri preferably but anyone will do really... <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1469674198ra/19843277.gif" width="300" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Secondly, I FOUND OUT HOW ANGELS WEAR THEIR SHIRTS! As you know from my last review this concept is really important to me and now that I've figured it out I need not read another word. Just kidding, this world is addicting. <br><br>I was a little unsure going into this book especially since one of the first scenes consisted of Raphael telling Elena to call him "Master" and explaining that she was simply his "pet".<br>Really, Raphael?! <b>
  <i>R.E.A.L.L.Y.</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1452526887ra/17704134.gif" width="350" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But I was pleasantly surprised. Within a few chapters the plot picked up and Raphael was more concerned about who was gruesomely executing angels and vampires and Lijuan's invitation to her creepy Ball of The Dead than beating his chest like a cave man. <br><br>The world was just as interesting as before and expanded passed Manhattan and into the Angelic city called the Refuge where baby angels were scolded for letting their wings drag, so cute, and more of the Angel's history revealed. I really love the world and the way the angels, vampires and humans interact is so unique - I can't wait to learn more! Once again Nalini Singh balanced perfectly between giving enough information where I wouldn't be confused but not too much as to give me a headache. <br><br>The plot was fast paced, exciting and was in no way took the back seat because of the romance. Though I did predict the final showdown, I have a feeling this was what the author wanted, there were a few other turns I didn't see coming. <br><br>There are a few things that differentiate a good book from a great book for me, minus the obvious one of a great plot, and those are: not only strong MCs but kickass secondary characters as well, details people DETAILS and no insta love.<br><br>One of my biggest pet peeves is insta love. I despise it. It's so unrealistic and instead of swooning I just find myself rolling my eyes and wanting to strangle the characters. I am all about the slow burn. Even though Raphael and Elena's situation was definitely more on the insta love side <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[with him turning her into an angel and all <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I actually didn't find it frustrating. They didn't instantly turn all gooey and heart eyed just because Elena <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[was now an angel <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. They were still at each other's throats and fighting each other to find equal ground to build their relationship on. I love a badass heroine, I mean who doesn't, but what I've come to notice in a lot of books is they begin to fade as soon as they hook up with the romantic interest. WHY! WHY DO AUTHORS DO THIS?! I was super nervous that Elena was going to begin to wilt as soon as her and Raphael got together, especially with the bit of insta love they had going on. But, she was just as badass as ever and though she did put up with a bit of BS, I thought it was BS but of course she thought it was so "hot", she did stand her ground and remain just as strong willed as in the first book. I loved watching their relationship bloom and the effort they had to put in to start trusting each other. Elena didn't lose herself in Rhapael and he stopped being SUCH a dick, still a little bit of a dick, and began to see Elena more than just a play thing. They still have a long way to go and I'm excited for watch their relationship progress.<br><br>That brings me to my next point: kickass MCs AND <b>SECONDARY CHARACTERS</b>! The secondary characters are just like.. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450039832ra/17370784.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>SO. SO. AWESOME.</b> <br><br>I seriously could not gush about them enough. Secondary characters are VERY important and I don't understand why some authors don't get this! Yeah, the main character is obviously the main focus but in my opinion a good writer puts in just as much effort into every character. Nalini Singh did such an amazing job I instantly feel in love with all of them, minus Sara she is boring. But Rhapael's Seven... <br><br>I LOVE THEM. Dmirti with his taunts and weird sexual preferences, Illium's jokes and friendship, Venom with his creepy snake eyes, poisoned filled fangs and ability to entice people and Naasir who was LITERALLY in like two pages and yet Nalini Singh made me LOVE HIM. AND THAT'S ONLY FOUR OF THEM! Okay, I have to stop or else I will go on forever. All the characters, minus Sara, are so intriguing and I NEED to know more about them. <br><br>At first I felt a little dissatisfied with the ending. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[All this build up for Slater and then Elena just goes and cuts his head off within two seconds. But then I sat back and thought about it and decided that she couldn't have been more badass. Here was the ancient Angel trying to taunt and scare her by bringing back to life the person who murdered her family and she just calming asks Aodhan for his sword turns around and beheads Slater stating that the gift "wasn't her taste". In front of all the ancient Angels like its no big deal even thought she is freaking out inside. Props to you, Elena! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>That brings me to my last point, I swear. I love that even though Nalini Singh's characters are badass immortals or kickass hunters they are very real. They have nightmares and insecurities and it makes them easier to relate to. Things aren't always rainbows and butterflies and Nalini Singh isn't afraid to cause her characters turmoil.<br> <br>Everything about this series so far is so well developed and detailed it's obvious how much love and effort Nalini Singh put into this story.<br><br>I know this review was really long so here a pic of a "hot male angel" as a reward for reading my review. Courtesy of Google. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1469688428i/19844424.gif" width="250" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>BAHAHAHAHA. I'M DYING!!<br>And that's not even the worst one..<br>Okay, I'm off to devour Archangel's Consort!</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="16111008498357216092" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <br/>
<br/><br/><b><br/>First time round I gave it 4 Stars now it is worth 5 Stars.<br/>5 “We die...... We die together. That's the deal.” Stars. <br/><br/>This book picks up shortly after the battle between Raphael and Uram. Elena is at the Ref</b></span>
  <span id="freeText5639143407142448637" style="display:none">
  <br>
  <a href="http://s39.photobucket.com/user/phoenix374/media/8255986_zpsmchhazcz.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1444557409i/16516918.jpg" alt=" photo 8255986_zpsmchhazcz.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
  <br>
<br><br><b><br>First time round I gave it 4 Stars now it is worth 5 Stars.<br>5 “We die...... We die together. That's the deal.” Stars. <br><br>This book picks up shortly after the battle between Raphael and Uram. Where nearly both died but where Raphael used a loophole making Elena the first made angel in history. An angel with a mortal heart.<br><br>Elena spent the last year in a coma and has to adjust to her new life. A life where her friends and family will die as she is no longer mortal. Elena is at the Refuge to get used to her wings and gets the 101 on how to be an angel/hunter. But even in the sanctuary of the angels brings trouble and trouble is attracted to Elena and in this book, it is no different. My favorite character of the book was the Sam the “baby angel” But also Bluebell as fantastic character. Such a joy to read his mischief side. <br>I didn’t expect the book to take place in the Refuge so much. But the story is well written. Ms. Singh knows how to write a story filled with suspense, action, steamy scenes and a battle of wills. That the angels/archangels do a lot for amusement and entertainment. There is always a price to pay.<br>We see how Raphael and Elena’s relationship develops and how the connection that they have develops even more. Which I loved now even more. Reading it for the second time I was still thoroughly sucked into the story when I read it the first time. <br>Raphael and Elena have been invited to China by the archangel Lijuan to celebrate Elena’s making. A ball is being held in her honor. Lijuan is evolving and she is becoming other. Which means nothing but problems for the Cadre. I personally think that she is going bat shit crazy.<br><br>Things that annoyed me where: <br><br>-Everyone still was tempted to kill Elena. This time it was fun to read. <br><br>-Everyone was saying having a mortal heart is a bad thing. Didn’t bother me at all. <br><br>-Raphael is becoming too mortal. He’s changing and that is what makes him even more appealing. <br><br>There were some things that I found to be repetitive. One of them being that of Elena’s past. Yes, that still bothers me although this time I get it more and see how it connects to her present.</b></span>

<div id="review_1230053534" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1230053534" />
    <a title="Angela" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4255477-angela"><img alt="Angela" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1398251387p2/4255477.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1230053534?book_show_action=true">Mar 17, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angela" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angela" href="/user/show/4255477-angela">Angela</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/8255986-archangel-s-kiss">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=2016-read">2016-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=poc">poc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=aoc">aoc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=kindle">kindle</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1230053534" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13912441410622271674">September 2016 Re-read - Buddy read with Maru, Aly, and Sarah: I'm always caught up in the story that's unfolding in Nalini Singh's books - and that hasn't changed here. Though I am getting a little less ... <i>accepting</i> of all the sexy times going on. I don't know, it's just not my thing. I skim and skim and skim those sections. And I can't blame Elena for being attracted to Raphael, but I want more story and less obsessing over him. I'm not complaining, really I'm not. I love these books, a lot. </span>
  <span id="freeText13912441410622271674" style="display:none">September 2016 Re-read - Buddy read with Maru, Aly, and Sarah: I'm always caught up in the story that's unfolding in Nalini Singh's books - and that hasn't changed here. Though I am getting a little less ... <i>accepting</i> of all the sexy times going on. I don't know, it's just not my thing. I skim and skim and skim those sections. And I can't blame Elena for being attracted to Raphael, but I want more story and less obsessing over him. I'm not complaining, really I'm not. I love these books, a lot. I just had to point it out because it's something that's changed in my personal reading tastes.<br /><br />I do love how their relationship progresses. I like that it's not easy and that they're learning how to be together, how to be a couple. I also love the storyline. <br /><br />And I'm really glad that we get back to New York, and Elena's circle of friends, in the next book.<br /><br /><br />Original review: I think I start every single review I do for Nalini Singh's books exclaiming how much she manages to impress me, how great it is, and how much I love it. <br /><br />This one is no different. Archangel's Kiss proves, once again, that Nalini Singh is a master at writing. She deftly weaves multiple storylines together, builds interest in supporting characters, and gives yet more depth to Raphael and Elena. <br /><br />Archangel's Kiss picks up a little over a year after Angels' Blood (the first full-length novel in the Guild Hunters series). Elena's spent that time in a healing coma, and has just woken as a newly Made angel. One who doesn't know how to be an angel, and has to learn everything - even those things she once knew, like how to fight. <br /><br />And she must learn quickly. The other angels, and archangels, have taken an interest in her. She's like a shiny new toy. One that someone is anxious to see how quickly they can break, hoping to take their place with the Cadre by that show of power. Refuge, a safe place for the angels, is suddenly no longer safe as attacks begin to happen, one after the other. Circling the threat closer and closer to Elena. <br /><br />Then there's Lijuan. The eldest of the archangels has taken a deadly interest in Elena, and is throwing a ball in her honor at the Forbidden City in Beijing. While rumors of her making the dead walk as living flourish, there's danger in accepting, but even more in refusing. Because this is not a social gathering to congratulate Elena, it's all about power. Testing Elena's and Raphael's, and Lijuan showing hers. Making it an invitation that can't be refused. <br /><br />Archangel's Kiss held me in a sort of thrall from the first word, to the last. We see Elena training with Raphael's Seven to get her up to speed, and work closer towards that first flight. The details in every page painted a clear picture of how the angels live. From their shirts, to their houses, to the beauty of flight. The action and mystery of the plot sped the story along, compelling me to not put my Kindle down until I hit the last sentence. There were many light moments to offset the growing darkness that surrounded and threatened them, including fields blooming in winter, a class with angel-children, and playful teasing with Illium. And, of course, there was the not-so-light heat and chemistry between Elena and Raphael. The sexual tension that builds between them is mind-blowing. <br /><br />Nalini deftly delves into the relationship of Elena and Raphael, showing the gradual growth and trust build between them beautifully and realistically. Their respective histories begin to unfold for us, and them. There are the horrors that hide in Elena's mind, even from her, and Raphael's past complete with the secret of his parents. Both of them were in unfamiliar territory, but they worked through it. With each other. And for each other. I can't think of anything more romantic than that. <br /><br />Raphael said that Elena would intrigue him through eternity. I think it's safe to say that this series will intrigue me for just as long. I'm fascinated with the world, and the characters that populate it. I feel as though I've been given the gift of seeing the world Nalini's created, and it's left me breathless for the next installment.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13912441410622271674" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1749152826" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1749152826" />
    <a title="Sarah" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3344685-sarah"><img alt="Sarah" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1388694025p2/3344685.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1749152826?book_show_action=true">Sep 05, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sarah" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sarah" href="/user/show/3344685-sarah">Sarah</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780575095748" href="/book/show/7307202-archangel-s-kiss">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=read-in-2016">read-in-2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=read-in-2011">read-in-2011</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=signed">signed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=books-i-own-print">books-i-own-print</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=read-in-2013">read-in-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=read-in-2020">read-in-2020</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=buddy-read">buddy-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=books-i-own-kindle">books-i-own-kindle</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1749152826" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5281144573141065533"><b>1st Read - May 2011</b><br/><b>2nd Read - March 2013</b><br/><b>3rd Read - September 2016</b><br/><b>4th Read - September 2020</b><br/><br/><b>Original Review</b><br/><br/>When Elena wakes up after a year long coma she is like a different person, her new abilities will only make her stronger in the long run but for now she is even more vulnerable than she was before. Raphael has taken her to the Refuge so she can continue her recovery but his enemies see her as his weak point and seek to destroy her. When mysterious murders start to occur it is Elena who has th</span>
  <span id="freeText5281144573141065533" style="display:none"><b>1st Read - May 2011</b><br /><b>2nd Read - March 2013</b><br /><b>3rd Read - September 2016</b><br /><b>4th Read - September 2020</b><br /><br /><b>Original Review</b><br /><br />When Elena wakes up after a year long coma she is like a different person, her new abilities will only make her stronger in the long run but for now she is even more vulnerable than she was before. Raphael has taken her to the Refuge so she can continue her recovery but his enemies see her as his weak point and seek to destroy her. When mysterious murders start to occur it is Elena who has the ability to track down the killer but can Raphael keep her safe?<br /><br />I loved the first book in this series (Angel's Blood) and was glad I already had a copy of Archangel's Kiss so I could continue Elena &amp; Raphael's journey immediately. I had high expectations for this book and Nalini Singh didn't disappoint me, if the rest of her books are as good as these 2 then she will be added to my list of must buy authors. This series continues to straddle the lines between paranormal romance and urban fantasy, the beginning of Archangel's Kiss was definitely more focused on the romance and then the action kicked into gear for the second half and left me breathless with anticipation. If you're a fan of either genre then I'm sure the series will have enough to keep you happy, my only recommendation would be to make sure you read the books in order but you should definitely read them!<br /><br />I love reading about Elena and Raphael and their relationship develops really nicely throughout the book. Raphael can come across as possessive and jealous but Elena also brings out his more caring and sensitive side and he is starting to learn that he can't force Elena into things, she has to choose to do them. Elena isn't used to having anyone to rely on, we saw in the first book how her father had rejected her after the deaths of her mother and sisters so know that she has had to stand on her own two feet. Although she is physically weaker than those around her she still shows great strength of character and refuses to show her fear. I was glad to find out more about her past and the events that lead her to become a Guild Hunter and I loved seeing her slowly learn to trust Raphael and start to open up to him.<br /><br />The world Nalini Singh has created is rich in detail and easy to picture, although her angels are hardly the benevolent creatures they are usually portrayed as they are fascinating to read about and we learn a lot more about their hierarchy in this book. Archangel's Kiss is a romantic, fast paced read that will have you hooked from the first page and leave you desperate for the next instalment. A highly recommended series but make sure you start with Angel's Blood!<br /><br />___________________<br /><br /><b>2nd Read</b><br /><br />I've really enjoyed my re-read of the first 2 Guild Hunter books. I never got past this point last time so I'm excited to read the rest of the series :o)<br /><br />___________________<br /><br /><b>3rd Read</b><br /><br />Rereading the entire Guild Hunter series with Aly, Ange &amp; Maru so that we're ready for the release of Archangel's Heart in November. <br /><br />I can't believe how much I'd forgotten about the earlier books and I'm appreciating the foreshadowing so much more this time around. Nalini is another author whose books just get better and better every time you read them.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5281144573141065533" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jonetta" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jonetta" href="/user/show/4876540-jonetta">Jonetta</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audio CD 9781400117161" href="/book/show/8041554-archangel-s-kiss">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4876540-jonetta?shelf=audiobook">audiobook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4876540-jonetta?shelf=buddy-read">buddy-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4876540-jonetta?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer303463953" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5644134564700176723">The story begins with Elena awakening from her coma after a year, learning she's now an angel, mated to Raphael. As she works to regain her strength, Elena must also adjust to her new circumstances, including her new body form, relationship with Raphael and a host of new enemies. And, Elena's memories of her family's devastation resurface throughout the story, sometimes at the most inopportune moments. <br/><br/>I loved the story's honesty. Yes, Elena and Raphael bring the heat but when things cool down, </span>
  <span id="freeText5644134564700176723" style="display:none">The story begins with Elena awakening from her coma after a year, learning she's now an angel, mated to Raphael. As she works to regain her strength, Elena must also adjust to her new circumstances, including her new body form, relationship with Raphael and a host of new enemies. And, Elena's memories of her family's devastation resurface throughout the story, sometimes at the most inopportune moments. <br /><br />I loved the story's honesty. Yes, Elena and Raphael bring the heat but when things cool down, they've got to figure out the routine of being a couple while learning to trust one another. His über alpha nature and her innate independence create friction as they jockey for position. It's not always happily ever after. <br /><br />We also learn so much more about angel "law" and the politics of the Archangels. There's lots of intrigue and excitement as the "heartless" angels recognize an opportunity, which is to take advantage of Elena's weakened condition. She's Raphael's Achille's heel for the moment and they're lining up. <br /><br />The narration worked for me as Justine Eyre has a sultry tone that befits both Raphael and Elena. Her character distinctions were wonderful. <br /><br />This was an exciting and interesting story and I'm now even more committed to continuing the series. </span>
  <a data-text-id="5644134564700176723" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText17391074766001904756" style="display:none"><b>The life and times of an angel made...</b><br /><br />Another winner from the <i>Romance Package</i> and a great opportunity to visit with my favourite hunter, angels, vampires and archangels.<br /><br />This instalment shows us that the strong can be temporarily incapacitated but can't be held down for long. The Hunter, Elena, wakes from a year-long nap with a few additional features and appendages. It takes a wee bit of adjustment, but she is determined to be strong and a hunter again...just one with wings. With a little help from her winged lover, Raphael, she will conquer her foes and climb the obstacles in her path.<br /><br />Plenty of action and adventure for these two with a few psychos playing games with the lives of humans, vampires and other angels. I'm thinking that a lot of those archangels have "issues". I think the power has gone to their heads and they may have lost a few brain cells.<br /><br />I again enjoyed this narrator and found her easy to listen to and follow.<br /><br />I will definitely be listening to more in this series, especially if it's in the Romance Package.</span>

Elena awakes after a year-long coma having been transformed into an archangel by Rafael in order to save her life. But now she must learn to live and fight in her new body--and fly, which is something of a disaster--all while the danger of LiTuan looms, an ancient archangel who has been raising the dead and wants Elena to die. <br/><br/>I loved the continued romance between Rafael and Elena, and it was also great to see more development </span>
  <span id="freeText3545832128692776732" style="display:none">This was a great continuation of Nalini Singh's guild hunter series. <div id="review_65540520" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/65540520" />
    <a title="Katie(babs)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/179852-katie-babs"><img alt="Katie(babs)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1242522005p2/179852.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/65540520?book_show_action=true">Jul 30, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katie(babs)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katie(babs)" href="/user/show/179852-katie-babs">Katie(babs)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer65540520" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8635270039334897954">In the mood for a dark, intense and smoldering sexy read that may have you gasping for breath? Nalini Singh delivers this in ways you can’t imagine with Archangel’s Kiss, the second book in her Guild Hunter Novel series. The first book, Angels Blood introduced vampire hunter Elena Deveraux, who lives in an alternate New York City universe where angels rule and are things of wonder to bow down to and be very afraid of. Elena was ordered to hunt down a supernatural serial killer than ended up bein</span>
  <span id="freeText8635270039334897954" style="display:none">In the mood for a dark, intense and smoldering sexy read that may have you gasping for breath? Nalini Singh delivers this in ways you can’t imagine with Archangel’s Kiss, the second book in her Guild Hunter Novel series. The first book, Angels Blood introduced vampire hunter Elena Deveraux, who lives in an alternate New York City universe where angels rule and are things of wonder to bow down to and be very afraid of. Elena was ordered to hunt down a supernatural serial killer than ended up being an archangel. The seductive and dangerous archangel that rules New York City, Raphael, is thousands of years old and has decided that Elena will be his new sexual pet. They engage in a battle of wits and an almost disturbing sexual dance as she hunted for this killer while Raphael hunted her at the same time.<br /><br />Angels Blood ended with Elena and Raphael killing the serial killer. Elena died from the outcome, but Raphael was able to save her. Now Elena is the first human in a millennia to be changed into an angel. Archangel’s Kiss begins after a year, where Elena was in a coma, has now awakened and is recovering, hidden away for her safety at the Refuge, where angels are all around her. Human are unaware of this place and only the angel’s vampire servants are welcomed. Elena, being hunter born is now an anomaly. She is very much like a new born, who’s learning to walk, or rather learning to fly. Raphael is there to help her, but their relationship, which is very new and scary, could go either way. Elena has come to love Raphael, the superior archangel who owns her heart, but Raphael is so used to taking what he wants and to treat Elena as his equal and not as a pet or a possession makes things very unstable between the two. Plus, there’s a possibility that Raphael could still kill her. <br /><br />Raphael is close to amoral as you can get and has lived many centuries as both a ruler and treated like a god. He longs to engage in mind numbing sex with his new angel mate, but because she’s still weak and his wild and brutal appetite could break her while they are intimate, he holds back. Raphael is quite the giver to the point where Elena may break any way because she’s so frustrated because of the way his foreplay (Raphael uses his fingers and mouth to give Elena satisfaction). Raphael has an elite group of warriors, called his Seven, which is a tight-knit group of vampires and angels who protect Raphael against any threats and danger. And now their most important responsibility is to protect Elena from being killed by Raphael’s fellow archangels, including Michaela, a very deranged and unstable archangel who despises Elena with a passion.<br /><br />As Elena goes through angel physical therapy, she keeps having nightmares about her mother’s and sisters’ brutal murders, as well as trying to understand why her father has turned his back on her. Also, one of the oldest archangel’s still living on Earth, Zhou Lijuan, has invited Elena to the Forbidden City. This invitation is a trap because Lijuan is creating a new race of undead, an army, where she can truly be a god in every sense of the word. Then angels and vampires are being brutally murdered, even angel children. And because of Elena’s special tracking powers, she’ll try to find this killer who may be in league with Lijuan. Elena must watch over her shoulder because she’s an easy target. And because Raphael’s feelings for Elena sometimes confuse him, he may lash out and become something he doesn’t want be. As long as Elena can love and accept him for who he is, they can be together for all eternity.<br /><br />Archangel’s Kiss is an amazing, well written, awesome world building book that I couldn’t put down. You can see how far Nalini has come with her writing and character building. She excels in writing such interesting characters, from Raphael who’s an amoral hero who walks a fine line into villainy, to Elena who puts all other urban fantasy/paranormal heroines to shame. The secondary characters of, Illium, a happy go lucky loving angel, is one that needs his own story. Even the near psycho Michaela with her questionable actions keeps the reader on their toes. <br /><br />There is so much going on with these pages. Intense is the perfect word when describing Archangel’s Kiss. The sensuality between Raphael and Elena is explosive and Nalini explains things she didn’t in Angels Blood. I really can’t find any faults except for the fact that the religious aspect is glazed over in regards to these angels. It may not be a big deal, but I would be interested in knowing more about these angel’s background, as in if there is a higher power ruling over these creatures and a Heaven and Hell, or they’re just a special society that always has been around.<br /><br />I would recommend you read Angels Blood first before Archangel’s Kiss. It introduces the world and characters why they act the way they do. Sometimes, I question how a supernatural couple can sustain their love in a believable way for hundreds or thousands of years? Nalini has given us proof that this is possible with Elena and Raphael. I’m already anxious to read their next installment. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="8635270039334897954" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer1716109712133771932">An interesting sophomore installment in the Guild Hunter series. There were some things I liked (great secondary cast, interesting villains), and some things I really didn't like (too much detail on lady juices, some repetitive things)... but overall, I thoroughly enjoyed this one. I really want some wings of my own. :) And I want to hug some of these broken secondary characters. </span>

<div id="review_743206768" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/743206768" />
    <a title="Jo" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14323468-jo"><img alt="Jo" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1434090906p2/14323468.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/743206768?book_show_action=true">Oct 17, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jo" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jo" href="/user/show/14323468-jo">Jo</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14323468-jo?shelf=book-boyfriend">book-boyfriend</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14323468-jo?shelf=mine">mine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14323468-jo?shelf=gr2013">gr2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14323468-jo?shelf=heroines-i-love">heroines-i-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14323468-jo?shelf=books-i-love">books-i-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14323468-jo?shelf=buddy-read">buddy-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14323468-jo?shelf=4-5-stars">4-5-stars</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer743206768" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8385228003038569837"><p>21/09/2016 Buddy read with the wonderful UF addicts over at BB&B</p> <blockquote>
  <i>I invite you to the Forbidden City, Raphael. Come, let us welcome this human you have embraced. Let us see the beauty of this connection between immortal and what was once mortal. I find myself fascinated for the first time in millennia.<br/>~ Zhou Lijuan</i>
</blockquote> <p>Hunter-born Elena Deveraux has just woken from a year-long coma, finding herself instead of broken, an angel. But her body is frail and wings are a lot more difficult to control th</p></span>
  <span id="freeText8385228003038569837" style="display:none"><p>21/09/2016 Buddy read with the wonderful UF addicts over at BB&amp;B</p> <blockquote>
  <i>I invite you to the Forbidden City, Raphael. Come, let us welcome this human you have embraced. Let us see the beauty of this connection between immortal and what was once mortal. I find myself fascinated for the first time in millennia.<br />~ Zhou Lijuan</i>
</blockquote> <p>Hunter-born Elena Deveraux has just woken from a year-long coma, finding herself instead of broken, an angel. But her body is frail and wings are a lot more difficult to control than she thought they would be. She needs a lot of training before she regains her strength and learns to fight with her wings, and how to fly. </p> <p>Archangel Raphael is used to be obeyed, and expects Elena to give him all the control in their relationship. But Elena is no puppet and she doesn’t do well with authority at all. They still have a long way to go in their relationship. </p> <p>But suddenly their time is cut short when archangel Lijuan decides to hold a ball in honor of Raphael’s recently made angel. And now Elena has mere weeks to get fight ready for the danger that awaits them at the Forbidden City. For Lijuan is ancient and her power over the dead has grown in the year Elena has been asleep. And the gift she has prepared for Elena is just what you would expect from an archangel without conscience. </p> <blockquote>
  <i> “I’m hunter-born,” she told him, the words husky. “I’ve never been safe.” </i>
</blockquote> <p>Elena is still as kick-ass as always. It was wonderful seeing her learn how to use her wings, not just for flying but learning how to fight with them. I love that she kept her hunter-born abilities, and the fact that they seem to have evolved a little. I’m also glad that she’s just as independent as always, and that she continues to stand up to Raphael when he’s being his dominating self. </p> <blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“I look into my heart and see the abyss looking back at me.”<br />“I won’t let you fall.” A fierce promise.<br />He held her close, his immortal with a mortal heart.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote> <p>Raphael is still just as arrogant as always, but he’s slowly learning that being with Elena is about giving not just taking. It says a lot about him that he fears losing himself, becoming the monster that archangels can be. And I do love that he appreciates the gift Elena gave him, by making him a little mortal. And I love how protective and possessive he is over her, it’s so damn sexy! </p> <blockquote><i>I’d say you were losing your innocence, but your nightmares tell me you lost that a long time ago.<br />Yes,</i> she admitted, giving him a glimpse of the most secret corner of her heart. <i>There was so much blood that day. I could see it on my skin even at the funeral. </i></blockquote> <p>Little by little we learn more about Elena and Raphael’s tragic pasts. I love that they are slowly opening up to each other, telling their secrets, their hurts. A lot was revealed about Elena’s brutal past, and I love that Raphael is always there to hold her after each nightmare. </p> <blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>So quickly she’d twined around his heart, becoming the most vital part of his existence. </b>
  </i>
</blockquote> <p>The romance continues to be fantastic! I love that they are slowly learning more about each other. The slow pace of their relationship is more realistic than the whirlwind of before. They need time to learn to trust each other, to give deeper meaning to the intense need, love and possessiveness they already have. The intense chemistry between them continues to scorch the pages, and I just love how much they want and need each other. </p> <blockquote>
  <i>Because while angels might be predators, it was the archangels who sat at the top of the food chain.</i>
</blockquote> <p>The more we learn about angels and archangels, the more I realise how cruel, vicious and inhumane they truly are. The angel politics continue to intrigue me, especially when you consider how little most things mean to them, except for their one supreme law <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[children are not to be harmed. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> It makes me hope that there is good in some of them. The place Elena was taking to recover, to learn about being an angel was amazing, and I loved learning more about angels. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[And the angel children were awesome, especially little Sam. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></p> <p>We finally meet the last members of Raphael’s Seven, Galen, Naasir and Aodhan, and I must say Illium is still my favorite, and Venom continues to fascinate me. Nalini teases us by giving us little pieces of information about all of them, which makes me even more eager to find out more. </p> <p>The plot in this book was excellent, and things got really interesting once they reached the Lijuan’s territory. Lijuan is so creepy, so terrifying and her reborn horrific. The fighting scenes were excellent, and I can’t wait to see what will happen next. </p> <p>Another fantastic instalment from my favorite author. I love this unique world that Ms. Singh created, it’s fascinating and the romance fantastic. Highly recommended.</p></span>
  <a data-text-id="8385228003038569837" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('KtQlUpae1U3a5snDehQilD5fB5bsOtlRXxHa6QNYYtxf37P1ng730Ez5vwbc0Hq43afgEYgwdDuX0ZObRWwI9Q==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('gnQHwykF3DnBXYQpL63La0DHRLZ3xvvKpLC9X9APi7n3f5FkIZX+pFdC8uyJaZNHoz+jMRPMVqBscPQtljvhkA==')})
  }
//]]>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer5038299962179812219">I've been writing as long as I can remember and all of my stories always held a thread of romance (even when I was writing about a prince who could shoot lasers out of his eyes). I love creating unique characters, love giving them happy endings and I even love the voices in my head. There's no other job I would rather be doing. In September 2002, when I got the call that Silhouette Desire wanted t</span>
  <span id="freeText5038299962179812219" style="display:none">I've been writing as long as I can remember and all of my stories always held a thread of romance (even when I was writing about a prince who could shoot lasers out of his eyes). I love creating unique characters, love giving them happy endings and I even love the voices in my head. There's no other job I would rather be doing. In September 2002, when I got the call that Silhouette Desire wanted to buy my first book, Desert Warrior, it was a dream come true. I hope to continue living the dream until I keel over of old age on my keyboard.<br /><br /><br />I was born in Fiji and raised in New Zealand. I also spent three years living and working in Japan, during which time I took the chance to travel around Asia. I’m back in New Zealand now, but I’m always plotting new trips. If you’d like to see some of my travel snapshots, have a look at the Travel Diary page (updated every month).<br /><br />So far, I've worked as a lawyer, a librarian, a candy factory general hand, a bank temp and an English teacher and not necessarily in that order. Some might call that inconsistency but I call it grist for the writer's mill.<br /><br /></span>
